2224 
2225 Int_t MiniTree::GetEntry(Long64_t entry)
2226 {
2227 // Read contents of entry.
2228  if (!fChain) return 0;
2229  return fChain->GetEntry(entry);
2230 }
2231 Long64_t MiniTree::LoadTree(Long64_t entry)
2232 {
2233 // Set the environment to read one entry
2234  if (!fChain) return -5;
2235  Long64_t centry = fChain->LoadTree(entry);
2236  if (centry < 0) return centry;
2237  if (fChain->GetTreeNumber() != fCurrent) {
2238  fCurrent = fChain->GetTreeNumber();
2239  Notify();
2240  }
2241  return centry;
2242 }

2247  // The Init() function is called when the selector needs to initialize
2248  // a new tree or chain. Typically here the branch addresses and branch
2249  // pointers of the tree will be set.
2250  // It is normally not necessary to make changes to the generated
2251  // code, but the routine can be extended by the user if needed.
2252  // Init() will be called many times when running on PROOF
2253  // (once per file to be processed).

3339 Bool_t MiniTree::Notify()
3340 {
3341  // The Notify() function is called when a new file is opened. This
3342  // can be either for a new TTree in a TChain or when when a new TTree
3343  // is started when using PROOF. It is normally not necessary to make changes
3344  // to the generated code, but the routine can be extended by the
3345  // user if needed. The return value is currently not used.
3346 
3347  return kTRUE;
3348 }
